different_country_flags_category = {
	#AFG
	AFG_reset_flag = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		
		cost = 0
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

		allowed = {
			original_tag = AFG
		}
		visible = {
			original_tag = AFG
			has_elections = yes
			
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = TAL
				has_cosmetic_tag = AFG
				AND = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = AFG_REB
					has_civil_war = yes
				}
				AND = { 
					has_cosmetic_tag = AFG_REB_S
					has_civil_war = yes
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision AFG_reset_flag"
			set_cosmetic_tag = AFG
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag
		}
	}
	
	
	AFG_Autocracy_flag = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		
		cost = 0
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

		allowed = {
			original_tag = AFG
		}

		visible = {
			original_tag = AFG
			has_elections = no
			OR = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = western_Western_Autocracy
				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
				has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy
			}
			NOT = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = AFG_AUTH		
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = AFG_REB_S
						AFG = { has_cosmetic_tag = AFG_AUTH }
					}
					has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy
					has_civil_war = yes
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision AFG_Autocracy_flag"
			set_cosmetic_tag = AFG_AUTH
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag
		}
	}
	
	AFG_Special_flag = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		
		cost = 0
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

		allowed = {
			original_tag = AFG
		}

		visible = {
			original_tag = AFG
			has_elections = no
			OR = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Kingdom
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Monarchist
				
				AND = {
					has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Communism
					has_civil_war = no
				}
				
				AND = {
					has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Communist-State
					has_civil_war = no
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = AFG_AUTH_S
				}
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision AFG_Special_flag"
			set_cosmetic_tag = AFG_AUTH_S
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag
		}
	}

	AFG_Rebel_flag = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		
		cost = 0
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

		allowed = {
			original_tag = AFG
		}

		visible = {
			original_tag = AFG
			has_civil_war = yes
			NOT = {
				tag = AFG
				has_cosmetic_tag = AFG_REB
				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Communist-State
				has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Communism
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy
				
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Fascism
				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Vilayat_e_Faqih
				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Mod_Vilayat_e_Faqih
				has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Kingdom
				has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Caliphate
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Monarchist
			}
			OR = {
				AFG = { has_cosmetic_tag = AFG_AUTH }
				
				AND = {
					AFG = { has_cosmetic_tag = AFG }
					NOT = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = western_Western_Autocracy
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy
					}
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision AFG_Rebel_flag"
			set_cosmetic_tag = AFG_REB
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag
		}
	}

				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Mod_Vilayat_e_Faqih
				has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Kingdom
				has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Caliphate
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Monarchist
			}
			OR = {
				BLR = { has_cosmetic_tag = BLR_AUTH }
				
				AND = {
					BLR = { has_cosmetic_tag = BLR }
					NOT = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = western_Western_Autocracy
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy

		}

			has_elections = no
			OR = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Kingdom
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Monarchist
				
				AND = {
					has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Communism
					has_civil_war = no
				}
				
				AND = {
					has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Communist-State
					has_civil_war = no
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = CBD_AUTH_S
				}
			}

				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy

						EGY = { has_cosmetic_tag = EGY_AUTH }

					has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

		allowed = {
			original_tag = JAP
		}

		visible = {
			original_tag = JAP
			has_elections = no
			OR = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Fascism
				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Vilayat_e_Faqih
				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Mod_Vilayat_e_Faqih
			}
			NOT = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = JAP_AUTH_SS

			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag
		}

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		
		cost = 0
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}

		allowed = {
			original_tag = JAP
		}

		visible = {
			original_tag = JAP
			has_civil_war = yes
			NOT = {
				tag = JAP
				has_cosmetic_tag = JAP_REB
				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Communist-State
				has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Communism
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy
				
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Fascism
				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Vilayat_e_Faqih
				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Mod_Vilayat_e_Faqih
				has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Kingdom
				has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Caliphate
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Monarchist
			}
			OR = {
				JAP = { has_cosmetic_tag = JAP_AUTH }
				
				AND = {
					JAP = { has_cosmetic_tag = JAP }
					NOT = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = western_Western_Autocracy
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy

				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Mod_Vilayat_e_Faqih
				has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Kingdom
				has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Caliphate
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Monarchist
			}
			OR = {
				KOR = { has_cosmetic_tag = KOR_AUTH }
				
				AND = {
					KOR = { has_cosmetic_tag = KOR }
					NOT = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = western_Western_Autocracy
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy
					}
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KOR_Rebel_flag"
			set_cosmetic_tag = KOR_REB
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag
		}

			has_elections = no
			OR = {
